Sight System, Ambidextrous Safety/Magazine Release, 10 Round Mag &amp; Includes Soft Case</span></strong></font></h2> <p><font style="color: #000000;" size="3" color="#ff0000"><strong><font size="2"><span>Built on a black polymer frame, aluminum slide with serrations and black anodized finish. Fixed white dot front sight and adjustable rear sight. Reversible blade allows selection of two white dots or black blade. Picatinny rail with multiple cross slots on underside of frame. Two interchangeable rubberized grips with serrations (no tools required to change). Ambidextrous manual safety, decocking lever and magazine release. Includes two 10-round magazines, two finger grip extension floorplates and soft case.</span></font><br></strong></font></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p class="p1"><font size="2">The Ruger SR22 Semi Auto Pistol is a do-it-all .22 pistol for shooters who really appreciate style and even small game hunting. It's currently my only pistol and it really is a "do-it-all" gun for me currently until I get enough $ to get a larger caliber pistol. Better than nothing at all. I wouldn't want to be shot by a few CCI Velocitors from it! That is the type ammo I keep it loaded with (40grain round nose hyper velocity) It has never jammed with any ammo I've ran thru it with the exception of American Eagle by Federal. Wouldn't eject it? So, It was the ammo, not the gun. I've put dozens of different brands thru it and it ate everything but AE by Federal. Even nasty 25 year old CCI ammo my Dad gave me. Feels great in the hand, very accurate, realiable, easy takedown, 2 mags come with it, what is there not to love about this thing?
